 New Delhi: a seminar on 'nirankar Dev Sevak and Bal Sahitya' was organized by Sahitya Akademi on the occasion of the birth anniversary of noted writer and child litterateur Nirankar Dev Sevak
 kaarykram main mukhya atithi ke rup main udghaatan vaktavy prakhyat kavi evam bal sahityakar bal swaroop raahi ne diya
 In this program, the seed statement was to be given to the child litterateur Prakash Manu, but he could not come due to accidental injury
 atah unka beej vaktavy shyaam susheel dwaara prastut kiya gaya
 Nirankar Dev Sevak's daughter-in-law and noted musician Poonam Sevak were specially present as special guests on the occasion
 swaagat vaktavy sahitya academy ke sachiv ke shrinivasrav ne diya
 While giving the opening statement, Bal Swaroop Rahi said that Indian children's literature does not need to be looked down upon
 bhartiya bal sahitya vishwa ke kisi bhi desh ke shreshth bal sahitya ke samakaksh he
 He said that child literature must have two characteristics so that the feelings and desires of the child mind can be revealed
 hamen bacchon ke liye upadesh dene kii bajaay sandesh dene kii koshish kerani chahie
 He said that the poems of the servant have both the feelings and desires of the children and each line of their poems is rhyme, they are not monotonous anywhere
 nirankaar dev sevak ji kii putravadhu ne unke jivan se jude kai maarmik prasang shrotaaon se saajha karte hue unki dincharya se jude kai prasangon ko prastut kiya
 He said that he lived a very simple life
 prakaash manu kii anupasthiti main unka beej vaktavy padhaa gaya, jisamen unhone kaha ki sevak keval bal kavitaayen likhte hi nahin the, balki ve bacchon ke saral, jigyaasu man or bal kavita ke marm, donon ko hi bahut gaharaai se samajhate the
 That is why in the post-independence period, he was by nature one of the most loved and favorite poets of children, whose poems echoed from village to village
 bachche jane-anjaane unhen gaate-gunagunaate the or aanandit ho uthte the
 Manu's statement was that many generations of children grew up dancing and singing along with the poems of the servant
 in kavitaaon se hi unhone jivan ke bade-bade paath siikhe
 Also, the art of living childhood with joy, unique fun and unique colors
 aage unhone kaha ki sevak ne apane yug ke anya bal sahityakaron kii tarah keval bacchon ke liye likhaa hi nahin, balki bal sahitya ko sahi disha dene kaa bada chunautibhara kaam bhi kiya
 He is a big and respected child litterateur, as well as a guide and era-maker of children's literature
 or donon hi morachon par unka yogadan laasaani he
 Welcoming everyone at the beginning of the program, Secretary of Sahitya Academy
 shrinivasrav ne kaha ki sahitya academy bal sahitya kaa mahatva bhalee-bhanti samajhati he or uske vikaas ke liye satat prayatnsheel he
 He also mentioned the work being done by the Sahitya Academy for the promotion of children's literature
 sangoshtee ke pratham satr main ‘nirankaar dev sevak evam bal kavita’ vishay par vichaar-vimarsh hua
 The session was chaired by eminent poet and child litterateur Divik Ramesh and Kamlesh Bhatt 'kamal', Jagdish Vyom and Rajinikanth Shukla presented their articles
 apane adhyakshiya bhaashan main divik ramesh ne kaha ki bal sahitya bacchon kii aawaaj he or hamen uskaa usee tarah se sammaan or pyaar karnaa chahie jaisaaki ham bacchon ko karte hai
 Divik Ramesh praised the poems written by the servant understanding the psychology of children and said that children are always dear to freedom, so we child writers should write poems for them only while respecting their tendency
 unhone bacchon ke mata-pita se bhi bal sahitya padhane kii apil karte hue kaha ki isse jahaan ve apane bacchon ke manovigyaan ko achche se samaj paayenge saath hi unke liye achche bal sahitya kaa chayan bhi kar paayenge
 In the second session of the seminar, the topic of 'nirankar Dev Sevak's thoughts and children's literature' was discussed
 is satr kii adhyakshata prakhyat lekhak sudhir vidhyaarthee ne kii or shakuntla kalra, ushaa yadav evam shyaam susheel ne apane aalekh prastut kiye
 The president of the session, Sudhir Vidyarthi, said that there should be an overall assessment of Nirankar Dev Sevak
 hamane unke bal sahitya kii to charchaa kii he lekin unke dwaara likhe gaye mahatvapurn praudh sahitya ko andekha kiya he
 The poems, editorials and other columns written by him are also unique and need to be considered
 kaarykram main kai mahatvapurn bal sahityakar or lekhak upasthit the
 The program was moderated by Sahitya Akademi editor Anupam Tiwari
 saarvajanik taur par bachche ko stanpan karaane ko lekar abhi bhi samaaj kii soch sankuchit hi maani jaani chahie
